# W

[Back to index](index.md)

## wab

### Sense 1: lexicon

- **Pronunciation:** `WAB`
- **Part of speech:** verb
- **Definition:** to wall, enclose, or make boundary
- **Register/status:** plain; accepted
- **Domains:** daily-life, technology-software, art-beauty, economics-provision, travel-place
- **Root family:** `WB`; Building/making; wall, enclosure, protective boundary; wall, enclosure, protective boundary
- **Pattern:** verb
- **Literal:** W-B root, action vowel a
- **Example:** Na wab.
- **Corpus:** unattested (0 attestations)

- **Pronunciation:** `WALADAX`
- **Part of speech:** verb
- **Definition:** to wildfire, burn through landscape, or manage uncontrolled fire
- **Register/status:** plain; accepted
- **Domains:** nature-ecology, travel-place, science-math
- **Root family:** `WLDX`; Nature; wildfire, landscape-burning disturbance; wildfire, uncontrolled landscape fire, burning disturbance across land
- **Pattern:** verb
- **Literal:** W-L-D-X root, action vowel a
- **Example:** Na waladax.
- **Corpus:** unattested (0 attestations)

- **Pronunciation:** `WARAH-LEK`
- **Part of speech:** noun
- **Definition:** doctrine, theory, or explanatory frame of: warehouse, goods storehouse
- **Register/status:** plain; accepted
- **Domains:** daily-life, technology-software, art-beauty, economics-provision, travel-place
- **Root family:** `WRH`; Building/making; warehouse, goods storehouse; warehouse, stored goods house, provision reserve
- **Pattern:** doctrine
- **Literal:** W-R-H root, doctrine suffix -lek
- **Example:** Warah-lek lek e rih.
- **Corpus:** unattested (0 attestations)
